<td style="width:10%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;5.07</td>
<td style="font-family:Arial;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Submission of Matters to a Vote of Security Holders.</td></tr></table> <p style="font-family:Arial;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">The Annual Meeting of Shareholders of Apple Inc. was held on February&#160;26, 2020. At the Annual Meeting, Apple&#8217;s shareholders voted on the following six proposals and cast their votes as described below.</p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt"></p>
<table cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" border="0" style="font-family:Arial;border-collapse:collapse;text-align:left;width:100%;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;border:0;">
